ramleh april

We left beyrout morn d our caravan consist three
hors three mule donkey charg two men dervish
erect blackbeard impass mussulman mustapha
pictur patienc goodnatur He born smile
face never abl chang express they

would defi santa Fe trader excel the anim less
interest master our hors sure slow plod
